MPESB Group 1 Sub Group 3 Online Form 2025 (Admit Card)
üîó ‚Ä¢

MP ESB Group-1 (Sub Group -3) Combined Recruitment Test - 2024 Various Post Recruitment 2025

Madhya Pradesh Employee Selection Board (MPESB)

Short Details of Notification MPPEB Group 1 Sub Group 3 Exam 2025

Important Dates

  • Application Begin: 25/02/2025
  • Last Date for Apply Online: 11/03/2025
  • Pay Exam Fee Last Date: 11/03/2025
  • Correction Last Date: 16/03/2025
  • Exam Date Start: 15/05/2025
  • Admit Card Available: Before Exam

Application Fee

  • General / Other State: 560/-
  • SC / ST / OBC: 310/-
  • Portal Charge: 60/- (Include)

  • Pay the Exam Fee Through Cash at KIOSK Or Pay Debit Card, Credit Card, Net Banking Fee Mode Only

Eligibility

  • Age Limit as on 01/01/2024

  • Minimum Age: 18 Years.
  • Maximum Age: 40 Years.

Age relaxation as per rules of MPPEB Group 1 Sub Group 3 Exam 2025 .

Short Details of Notification RSSB NHM Advt No. : 01/2025

Important Dates

  • Application Begin: 02/04/2025
  • Last Date for Apply Online: 01/05/2025
  • Pay Exam Fee Last Date: 01/05/2025
  • RSSB NHM Exam Date: As per Schedule
  • Admit Card Available: Before Exam

Application Fee

  • General / OBC: 600/-
  • OBC NCL: 400/-
  • SC / ST: 400/-
  • Correction Charge: 300/-

  • This fee is for one time registration, now after paying the OTR fee once, the candidate will not have to pay the application fee again and again.

  • Pay the Exam Fee Through Emitra CSC Center, Debit Card, Credit Card, Net Banking.

Eligibility

  • Age Limit as on 01/01/2026

  • Minimum Age: 21 Years
  • Maximum Age: 40 Years

BHU Junior Clerk Recruitment 2025

Banaras Hindu University (BHU)

Short Details of Notification BHU Junior Clerk Advt No : 07/2024-2025

  • Application Begin: 18/03/2025
  • Last Date for Apply Online: 17/04/2025
  • Pay Exam Fee Last Date: 17/04/2025
  • Submit Form Hard Copy: 22/04/2025
  • Exam Date: As per Schedule
  • Admit Card Available: Before Exam

Application Fee

  • General / OBC / EWS: 500/-
  • SC / ST: 0/-
  • All Category Female: 0/-

  • Pay the Exam Fee Through Debit Card / Credit Card / Net Banking / UPI Fee Mode Only.

  • Maximum Age: 30 Years

RSMSSB Rajasthan Fourth Class Employee Recruitment 2025

Rajasthan Staff Selection Board (RSSB) | RSMSSB

Short Details of Notification Rajasthan 4th Grade Employee Advt No. : 19/2024

  • Application Begin: 21/03/2025
  • Last Date for Apply Online: 19/04/2025
  • Complete Form Last Date: 19/04/2025

  • SC / ST: 400/-

  • Maximum Age: 40 Years

Short Details of Notification UPPSC Mains 2024

Application Fee

  • General / OBC: 225/-
  • SC / ST: 105/-
  • PH Candidates: 25/-

  • Fees Details Are Tentative

  • Maximum Age: 40 years

Age relaxation as per rules of UPPSC Mains 2024.

  • ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§ö‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§≠‡§µ‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§®‡§ø‡§ß‡§ø ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§ó‡§†‡§® ‡§≠‡§æ‡§∞‡§§ ‡§∏‡§∞‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∂‡•ç‡§∞‡§Æ ‡§è‡§µ‡§Ç ‡§∞‡•ã‡§ú‡§ó‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§Æ‡§Ç‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§≤‡§Ø -‡§ï‡•á ‡§Ö‡§Ç‡§§‡§∞‡•ç‡§ó‡§§ ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§Ø‡§∞‡§§ ‡§µ‡•à‡§ß‡§æ‡§®‡§ø‡§ï ‡§®‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§Ø ‡§π‡•à ‡§ú‡§ø‡§∏‡§ï‡§æ ‡§â‡§¶‡•ç‡§¶‡•á‡§∂‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§ö‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§≠‡§µ‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§®‡§ø‡§ß‡§ø ‡§è‡§µ‡§Ç ‡§µ‡§ø‡§µ‡§ø‡§ß ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§µ‡§ß‡§æ‡§® ‡§Ö‡§ß‡§ø‡§®‡§ø‡§Ø‡§Æ, 1952 ‡§ï‡•á ‡§§‡§π‡§§ ‡§®‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞‡§ø‡§§ ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ú‡§ø‡§ï ‡§∏‡•Å‡§∞‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§æ ‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ú‡§®‡§æ‡§ì‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡§®‡•ç‡§µ‡§Ø‡§® ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§á‡§∏ ‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ú‡§®‡§æ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§Ö‡§Ç‡§§‡§∞‡•ç‡§ó‡§§ ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§∏‡•ç‡§•‡§æ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§ö‡§æ‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§≠‡§µ‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§®‡§ø‡§ß‡§ø, ‡§™‡•á‡§Ç‡§∂‡§® ‡§è‡§µ‡§Ç ‡§¨‡•Ä‡§Æ‡§æ ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§¨‡§Ç‡§ß‡•Ä ‡§≤‡§æ‡§≠ ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§¶‡§æ‡§® ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡•á ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§

Promotion or Ads on Whatsapp Channel Terms
üîó ‚Ä¢ Terms & Conditions for WhatsApp Promotion

Terms & Conditions for WhatsApp Promotion

1. Posting Duration:

The post/link you provide will be shared on our channel for a fixed duration of 24-48 hours only.

2. Right to Update New Posts:

30 minutes after your post or link is shared, we reserve the right to update new posts on our channel.

3. Post Removal:

Once the specified duration ends, your post/link will be removed from our channel.

  • ‡§∏‡§Æ‡§ó‡•ç‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§à‡§°‡•Ä ‡§è‡§ï ‡§µ‡§ø‡§∂‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü ‡§™‡§π‡§ö‡§æ‡§® ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§ñ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ (Unique ID) ‡§π‡•à ‡§ú‡•ã ‡§Æ‡§ß‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§¶‡•á‡§∂ ‡§∏‡§∞‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•ç‡§µ‡§æ‡§∞‡§æ ‡§®‡§æ‡§ó‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§¶‡§æ‡§® ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§Ü‡§à‡§°‡•Ä ‡§∞‡§æ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§ï‡•á ‡§®‡§æ‡§ó‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§µ‡§ø‡§≠‡§ø‡§®‡•ç‡§® ‡§∏‡§∞‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ú‡§®‡§æ‡§ì‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•á‡§µ‡§æ‡§ì‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§≤‡§æ‡§≠ ‡§â‡§†‡§æ‡§®‡•á ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡§¶‡§¶ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§

üîó ‚Ä¢ Apaar ID Card Download

Apaar ID Card Download

The APAAR ID card, also known as the One Nation One Student ID, is a unique 12-digit identification number for students in India. It's designed to digitally store and manage all academic credits, including scorecards, mark sheets, degrees, diplomas, and certificates.

üì¢ APAAR ID Card ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä
